					has_country_modifier = gme_padmasambhava_hidden_valley1
					has_country_modifier = gme_padmasambhava_hidden_valley2
					has_country_modifier = gme_padmasambhava_hidden_valley3
				}
			}
			remove_country_modifier = gme_padmasambhava_hidden_valley1
			remove_country_modifier = gme_padmasambhava_hidden_valley2
			remove_country_modifier = gme_padmasambhava_hidden_valley3
		}

					owner = {
						has_country_flag = dependencylost
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				remove_country_modifier = gme_potala_palace1
				remove_country_modifier = gme_potala_palace2
				remove_country_modifier = gme_potala_palace3
			}

				has_country_flag = subjectmonumentlost
				 OR = {

				}
			}
			remove_country_modifier = gme_potala_palace1
			remove_country_modifier = gme_potala_palace2
			remove_country_modifier = gme_potala_palace3
